\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{/* However, we still expose explicit release-\/acquire accessors so it */}    \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{/* can be made clear when they are required. */}                            \(\backslash\)}
